class=\"content-wrap\">\n            <div class=\"category-description\">Take a 360 degree tour of BCS, nestled in the hills of the Eastern Townships at the edge of the St. Francis River. Built in 1918, our 240-acre campus features historic buildings and comfortable residences. Visit our student centre, art studio, music room, dining hall, classrooms, indoor rink, double gym with climbing wall, and more.</div>\n\n        <ul class=\"no-bullets\">\n        <li class=\"group
